  - <span data-ttu-id="b2711-1897">**Data\_Doc\_AccessMode** – Dokument je samo za branje/ga je mogoče urejati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-1897">**Data\_Doc\_AccessMode -** Document is read only/editable</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="b2711-1898">**Data\_Doc\_AssistedReadingReasons** – Nabor vnaprej določenih vrednosti, zakaj je bil dokument odprt v načinu vodenega branja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-1898">**Data\_Doc\_AssistedReadingReasons -** Predefined set of values of why document was opened in assisted reading mode</span></span>

### <a name="application-status-and-boot-subtype"></a><span data-ttu-id="b2711-2172">*Stanje aplikacije in podvrsta zagona*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2172">*Application status and boot subtype*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b2711-2173">Določanje, ali je prišlo do specifičnih dogodkov funkcije, kot sta zagon ali zaustavitev, in funkcije, ki se izvaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2173">Determination if specific feature events have occurred, such as start or stop, and if feature is running.</span></span>

#### <a name="officeextensibilityofficejsappactivated"></a><span data-ttu-id="b2711-2174">Office.Extensibility.OfficeJS.Appactivated</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2174">Office.Extensibility.OfficeJS.Appactivated</span></span>

#### <a name="officepowerpointdocoperationopen"></a><span data-ttu-id="b2711-2399">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.Open</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2399">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.Open</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="b2711-2400">Ta dogodek je zbran vsakokrat, ko PowerPoint odpre datoteko.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2400">Collected whenever PowerPoint opens a file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b2711-2401">Vsebuje informacije o uspehu, podrobnosti o napaki, metriko učinkovitosti delovanja in osnovne podrobnosti o datoteki, vključno z vrsto oblike zapisa datoteke ter metapodatki dokumenta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2401">Contains success information, failure details, performance metrics, and basic details about the file including file format type and document metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b2711-2402">Te informacije so zahtevane, da PowerPoint lahko uspešno odpira datoteke in pri tem ne izgublja na učinkovitosti delovanja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2402">This information is necessary to ensure PowerPoint can open files successfully with no degradation in performance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b2711-2403">Z njimi lahko diagnosticiramo težave, ki jih odkrijemo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2403">It allows us to diagnose any problems we discover.</span></span>

#### <a name="officewordfileopenopenffileopenxstzcore"></a><span data-ttu-id="b2711-2687">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenFFileOpenXstzCore</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2687">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenFFileOpenXstzCore</span></span>

#### <a name="officewordfileopenopenifrinitargs"></a><span data-ttu-id="b2711-2753">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenIfrInitArgs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2753">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenIfrInitArgs</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b2711-2754">Ta dogodek ponazarja, da Microsoft Office Word odpira dokument s pomočjo aktivacije modula COM ali ukazne vrstice.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2754">This event indicates Office Word opens a document via COM activation or command line.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b2711-2755">Prav tako vsebuje kritične podatke o učinkovitosti odpiranja datotek in z vidika uporabnika predstavlja dogodek za zagon aplikacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2755">It also contains critical file open performance data, and is an app start event from user perspective.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b2711-2756">Dogodek nadzira, ali funkcija »Odpri datoteko iz ukazne vrstice« deluje običajno.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2756">The event monitors whether file-open-from-command-line is working as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b2711-2757">Prav tako se uporablja za izračunane mesečne aktivne uporabnike/naprave in za metriko zanesljivosti v oblaku.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2757">It is also used to calculated monthly active users/devices, and cloud reliability metrics.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b2711-2758">Zbrana so sledeča polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2758">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="b2711-2759">**Data\_AddDocTelemRes** – Poroča, ali lahko pravilno dopolnimo druge vrednosti dogodka, povezane s telemetrijo dokumenta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2759">**Data\_AddDocTelemRes -** Reports whether we were able to properly populate other document telemetry related values in the event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b2711-2760">Uporablja se za diagnostiko kakovosti podatkov</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2760">Used for data quality diagnostics.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="b2711-2761">**Data\_BytesAsynchronous –** število bajtov (stisnjenih), za katerega menimo, da lahko odpremo datoteko brez tega števila, če jih pridobimo, preden uporabnik želi začeti urejati dokument oz. ga morda shraniti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2761">**Data\_BytesAsynchronous -** Number of bytes (compressed) that we believe we can open the file without if we get them before the user wants to start editing or maybe saving.</span></span>

#### <a name="officewordfileopenopenloadfile"></a><span data-ttu-id="b2711-2818">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenLoadFile</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2818">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenLoadFile</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b2711-2819">Ta dogodek ponazarja, da Microsoft Office Word odpira dokument s pomočjo pogovornega okna za odpiranje</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2819">This event indicates Office Word opens a document via Open dialog.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b2711-2820">Prav tako vsebuje kritične podatke o učinkovitosti odpiranja datotek in z vidika uporabnika predstavlja dogodek za zagon aplikacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2820">It also contains critical file open performance data, and is an app start event from user perspective.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b2711-2821">Dogodek nadzira, ali funkcija »Odpri datoteko s pogovornim oknom za odpiranje« deluje običajno.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2821">The event monitors whether file-open-from-the-open-file-dialog is working as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b2711-2822">Prav tako se uporablja za izračunane mesečne aktivne uporabnike/naprave in za metriko zanesljivosti v oblaku.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2822">It is also used to calculated monthly active users/devices, and cloud reliability metrics.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b2711-2823">Zbrana so sledeča polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2823">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="b2711-2824">**Data\_AddDocTelemRes** – Poroča, ali lahko pravilno dopolnimo druge vrednosti dogodka, povezane s telemetrijo dokumenta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2824">**Data\_AddDocTelemRes -** Reports whether we were able to properly populate other document telemetry related values in the event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b2711-2825">Uporablja se za diagnostiko kakovosti podatkov</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2825">Used for data quality diagnostics.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="b2711-2826">**Data\_BytesAsynchronous –** število bajtov (stisnjenih), za katerega menimo, da lahko odpremo datoteko brez tega števila, če jih pridobimo, preden uporabnik želi začeti urejati dokument oz. ga morda shraniti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2826">**Data\_BytesAsynchronous -** Number of bytes (compressed) that we believe we can open the file without if we get them before the user wants to start editing or maybe saving</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="b2711-2827">**Data\_BytesAsynchronousWithWork –** število bajtov (stisnjenih), pri katerem morda še lahko odpremo datoteko brez tega števila, vendar bi zato morali občutno spremeniti kodo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2827">**Data\_BytesAsynchronousWithWork -** Number of bytes (compressed) that we might be able to open the file without but would require significant code investments to make it happen</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="b2711-2828">**Data\_BytesSynchronous –** število bajtov (stisnjenih), ki ga moramo pridobiti, preden lahko odpremo datoteko</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2828">**Data\_BytesSynchronous -** Number of bytes (compressed) that we must have before we can start opening the file</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="b2711-2829">**Data\_BytesUnknown –** število bajtov v delih dokumenta, za katerega menimo, da ga ne bomo našli</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2829">**Data\_BytesUnknown -** Number of bytes in document parts that we don’t expect to find</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="b2711-2830">**Data\_DetachedDuration –** koliko časa je bila dejavnost ločena od niti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2830">**Data\_DetachedDuration -** How long was the activity detached from the thread</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="b2711-2831">**Data\_Doc\_AccessMode** – Dokument je samo za branje/ga je mogoče urejati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2831">**Data\_Doc\_AccessMode -** Document is read only/editable</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="b2711-2832">**Data\_Doc\_AssistedReadingReasons** – Nabor vnaprej določenih vrednosti, zakaj je bil dokument odprt v načinu vodenega branja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2832">**Data\_Doc\_AssistedReadingReasons -** Predefined set of values of why document was opened in assisted reading mode</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="b2711-2833">**Data\_Doc\_ChunkingType** – Enote, ki se uporabljajo za postopno odpiranje dokumenta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-2833">**Data\_Doc\_ChunkingType -** Units used for incremental document open</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="b2711-3421">**Data\_BlockedDriverVersion** – različica gonilnika na seznamu prepovedanih</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-3421">**Data\_BlockedDriverVersion** - Version of the driver that was blocklisted</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="b2711-3422">**Data\_UpdatedDriverVersion** – različica posodobljenega gonilnika</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-3422">**Data\_UpdatedDriverVersion** - Version of the updated driver</span></span>

#### <a name="officegraphicsspritememcorrupt"></a><span data-ttu-id="b2711-3423">Office.Graphics.SpriteMemCorrupt</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-3423">Office.Graphics.SpriteMemCorrupt</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b2711-3424">Prijavi vse napake, zaznane pri telemetriji za določanje pomnilnika za slike.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-3424">Reports any errors detected in the sprite memory accounting telemetry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b2711-3425">Ta dogodek je pomemben za ocenjevanje stanja telemetrije porabe grafičnega pomnilnika.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-3425">Critical for assessing health of the graphics memory usage telemetry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b2711-3426">Ti podatki so zahtevani za preverjanje, ali je naša telemetrija pomnilnika SpriteMem pravilna.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-3426">This information is needed to validate the correctness of our SpriteMem telemetry.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b2711-3427">Zbrana so sledeča polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-3427">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="b2711-3428">**Data\_CurrentSpriteMem** – skupna količina pomnilnika, ki je aktivno dodeljen za prikaz slik na zaslonu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-3428">**Data\_CurrentSpriteMem** - Total amount of memory that is actively allocated to hold sprites (images) that result in screen content.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="b2711-3429">**Data\_Function** – ime funkcije, ki poskuša sprostiti pomnilnik za slike</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-3429">**Data\_Function** - The name of the function that is attempting to release sprite memory.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="b2711-3430">**Data\_SpriteMemToRemove** – količina pomnilnika, ki bo odstranjena iz dodelitve za slike.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-3430">**Data\_SpriteMemToRemove** - Amount of memory to be removed from sprite allocation.</span></span>

#### <a name="officepowerpointpptsharednointernetconnectivity"></a><span data-ttu-id="b2711-3431">Office.PowerPoint.PPT.Shared.NoInternetConnectivity</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-3431">Office.PowerPoint.PPT.Shared.NoInternetConnectivity</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b2711-3432">Ti podatki so zbrani, kadar PowerPoint zazna, da ni internetne povezave.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-3432">Collected whenever PowerPoint detects there is no internet connectivity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b2711-3433">Microsoft uporablja te podatke za pridobivanje diagnostičnih informacij o internetni povezavi uporabnika, da lahko bolje razume učinek, kako to vpliva na povezljivost z Officeovimi storitvami.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-3433">Microsoft uses this data to get diagnostic information about the user's internet connection to be able to understand how that impacts connectivity to Office services.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b2711-3434">Zbrana so sledeča polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-3434">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="b2711-3435">**Data\_IsNexusDetected:bool** – prikaže, ali je stanje internetne povezave na voljo med klicanjem storitve Nexus (true) ali pri klicanju programskega vmesnika za splošno spletno storitev (false)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b2711-3435">**Data\_IsNexusDetected:bool** - shows whether we got the Internet connectivity status when calling Nexus service (value true) or when calling generic web service API call (value false)</span></span>
